  <div id="method-i-closest_point" class="method-detail ">

    <div class="method-heading">
      <span class="method-name">closest_point</span><span
        class="method-args">(point)</span>

      <span class="method-click-advice">click to toggle source</span>

    </div>

    <div class="method-description">

      <p>On cherche et retourne le point le plus proche de celui passé Cout : O(n),

    avec n le nombre d&#39;éléments dans notre Array de points @param [Point] point</p>

    <div class="method-source-code" id="closest_point-source">
  <pre><span class="ruby-comment"># File point_manager.rb, line 34</span>

    <span class=“ruby-keyword”>def</span> <span class=“ruby-identifier”>closest_point</span>(<span class=“ruby-identifier”>point</span>)

    <span class="ruby-comment"># On mémorise la distance pour éviter d&#39;avoir à la recalculer</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier">closest_point</span> = <span class="ruby-keyword">nil</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier">distance</span>      = <span class="ruby-value">0</span>

<span class="ruby-ivar">@points</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier">each</span> <span class="ruby-keyword">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier">pt</span><span class="ruby-operator">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier">tmp_distance</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier">point</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier">square_distance</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier">pt</span>)
  <span class="ruby-keyword">if</span> <span class="ruby-identifier">closest_point</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier">nil?</span> <span class="ruby-operator">||</span> <span class="ruby-identifier">tmp_distance</span> <span class="ruby-operator">&lt;</span> <span class="ruby-identifier">distance</span>
    <span class="ruby-identifier">closest_point</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier">pt</span>
    <span class="ruby-identifier">distance</span>      = <span class="ruby-identifier">tmp_distance</span>
  <span class="ruby-keyword">end</span>
<span class="ruby-keyword">end</span>

<span class="ruby-comment"># On retire le point de notre Array de points</span>
<span class="ruby-ivar">@points</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier">delete</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier">closest_point</span>)
<span class="ruby-comment"># On indique au point passé en paramètre la distance avec le point trouvé</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier">point</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier">distance_closest_point</span> =<span class="ruby-constant">Math</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier">sqrt</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier">distance</span>)

<span class="ruby-identifier">closest_point</span>

    <span class=“ruby-keyword”>end</span></pre>

        </div><!-- closest_point-source -->

  </div>

    <span class=“ruby-keyword”>def</span> <span class=“ruby-identifier”>generate</span>(<span class=“ruby-identifier”>number</span>)

    (<span class="ruby-value">1</span><span class="ruby-operator">..</span><span class="ruby-identifier">number</span>).<span class="ruby-identifier">each</span> {
  <span class="ruby-ivar">@points</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier">push</span>(<span class="ruby-constant">LinkedPoint</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier">new</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier">rand</span>(<span class="ruby-value">0.0</span><span class="ruby-operator">..</span><span class="ruby-value">1.0</span>), <span class="ruby-identifier">rand</span>(<span class="ruby-value">0.0</span><span class="ruby-operator">..</span><span class="ruby-value">1.0</span>)))
